Dear Purchasing Manager,

Greetings and trust you are well.

We are wet wipes manufacturer "Shandong Baihe Sanitary Products Co Ltd." - foucus on wet & dry wipes and Epidemic prevention products (mask and gloves) for 19 years.
For now, exporting is our biggest market and servicing for many big brands OEM production. Our factory services for many big traders in China, but deelpy hope to build direct relationship with you:)

We have over 1500 specifications functional wipes, 6 automatic lines, 22 semi-automatic lines, 280 experienced staffs and FDA, NDC, TUV whole factory certificated, ISO9001 certificates etc. So no matter quality control or output service, please trust we have ability and sincerity to be your best partner.

Besides, we have own mask production and very firm gloves partner factories(PVC and nitrile) which we sell each other - can maintain best price and delivery in China. Please feel free to let us know requirment and compare the price better.



As first email is quite easily to be blocked to junk box with attachment or webiste, we look forward to receiving your kind reply, then we can follow up our website, E-catalogue and other required documents accordingly.



Kind Regards,

Hello FSC members,
¬†
I apologize for the last-minute nature of this email, but it is also a somewhat urgent matter for any member firm with drivers that cross the border, that may not be aware of a last minute Order in Council.
According to Public Health Canada websites and confirmed by CTA/OTA (see links below):
¬†
ALL travellers (including essential workers, such as truck drivers) arriving at a Canadian border, by LAND, sea or air, as of Monday February 22nd MUST use the ‚ÄúArriveCAN‚Äù app on their smartphone (or online) PRIOR to reaching the border.
Unless, the government makes a last minute exception/exemption for truck drivers later today, drivers that do not use this app face both delays and fines starting Monday.
Essential workers do NOT need to prove they had a negative Covid test, nor to complete the quarantine portion, but MUST complete the contact info and self-assessment portions.
